wikipedia wikidata mismatch - follow wikipedia redirect - for subject prefixed tags
subject:wikidata and subject:wikipedia tags link to a different objects, because subject:wikipedia tag points to a redirect that should be followed
Q983030 vs (missing) article redirects from en:Theobald Mathew (temperance reformer) to en:Father Mathew
Theobald Mathew - an affected OSM element that may be improved

Q5167610 vs (missing) article redirects from en:Coombe Women & Infants University Hospital to en:The Coombe Hospital
Coombe Hospital Memorial - an affected OSM element that may be improved
